customVerifyCallback)` at line 181\\n\\n## Downstream (Server) Certificate Verification - Client Certificate Validation\\n\\nWhen Envoy acts as a server receiving connections, it verifies client certificates:\\n\\n1. **Configuration**: `source/extensions/transport_sockets/tls/downstream_config.cc` configures the downstream TLS context using `ServerContextConfigImpl`\\n2. **Socket Factory**:
